                  </form>, [or the former only accord. to the Mgh., as will be seen by what follows,] inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">قَدْرٌ</foreign>, (S, Msb,) is from <foreign lang="ar">التَّقْدِيرُ</foreign>, (S,) [or] it signifies the same as   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n35272-1" target="قدّرتُ" n="1" lang="ar" type="7" subtype="WOTF" select="n35272"/> الشَّىْءَ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَقْدِيرٌ</foreign>: (Msb:) [which latter phrase is afterwards mentioned in the S, but unexplained: the meaning is, <hi rend="ital">I measured the thing; computed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">determined, its quantity, measure, size, bulk, proportion, extent, amount, sum, limit</hi> or <hi rend="ital">limits,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">number:</hi>] <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n35272-2" target="قدّر" n="2" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar" select="n35273"/>الشَّىْءَ</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">he computed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">determined,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">computed by conjecture, the quantity, measure, size, bulk, proportion, extent, amount, sum,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">number, of the thing,</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">حَزَرَهُ</foreign>,) <hi rend="ital">in order that he might know how much it was.</hi> (IKtt.) It is said in a trad., <foreign lang="ar">إِذَا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">غُمَّ عَلَيْكُمُ الهِلَالُ فَٱقْدِرُوا لَهُ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">فَٱقْدُرُوا</foreign>; (S, Msb; *) or <foreign lang="ar">إِنْ غْمَّ عَلَيْكُمْ فَٱقْدِرُوا</foreign>, with kesr to the <foreign lang="ar">د</foreign>; (Mgh, Msb; *) for <foreign lang="ar">فَٱقْدُرُوا</foreign>, with damm, is wrong; (Mgh;) and Ks. say, that you say <foreign lang="ar">قَدَرْتُ الشَّىْءَ</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">أَقْدِرُهُ</foreign>, with kesr, and that he had not heard any other aor.: (TA:) the meaning of the trad. is, [<hi rend="ital">When the new moon</hi> (of Ramadán) <hi rend="ital">is hidden from you by a cloud or mist,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">if it be so hidden,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">compute ye</hi> (  
      <anchor/><foreign lang="ar"><ref cref="n35272-3" target="قَدِّرُوا" n="3" type="3" subtype="PO" lang="ar"/> </foreign>) <hi rend="ital">the number of the days to it,</hi> (Mgh, Msb,) and so complete Shaabán, making it thirty days: (S, * Mgh, * Msb:) or, as some say, <hi rend="ital">compute ye</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">قَدِّرُوا</foreign>) <hi rend="ital">the mansions of the moon, and its course in them</hi> [<hi rend="ital">to it,</hi> i. e., to the new moon]. (Msb.) See also 5.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence, app., the saying,] <foreign lang="ar">أُقْدُرْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بِذَرْعِكَ بَيْنَنَا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">See thou and know thy rank,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">estimation, among us.</hi> (AO.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  Hence also,] <foreign lang="ar">مَا قَدَرُوا ٱللّٰهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ</foreign> [Kur., vi. 91, and other places, meaning, <hi rend="ital">And they have not estimated God with the estimation that is due to Him:</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">and they have not magnified,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">honoured, God, with the magnifying,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">honouring, that is due to Him:</hi> (S, K:) for <foreign lang="ar">قَدْرٌ</foreign> signifies [also] <hi rend="ital">a magnifying,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">honouring:</hi> (K:) or <hi rend="ital">have not assigned to God the attributes that are due to Him:</hi> (Lth:) or <hi rend="ital">have not known what God is in reality.</hi> (El-Basáïr.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">قَدَرَ الشَّىْءَ بِالشَّىْءِ</foreign>, aor.                   <hi rend="ital">he measured,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">compared, the two things,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">cases, together;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">قَايَسَ</foreign>; (K, art. <foreign lang="ar">قيس</foreign>;) and so <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n35272-7" target="قَادَرَ" n="7" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>بَيْنَهُمَا</foreign>. (L, art. <foreign lang="ar">قيس</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  [Hence, app.,] <foreign lang="ar">قَدَرَ الأَمْرَ</foreign>, (L, K,) and <foreign lang="ar">إِلَى الأَمْرِ</foreign>, (L,) aor.
